******************************************************
*
* Enforcer spark code
*
* On entry:
*    U - pointer to thread element
*
* On exit:
*    A - delay until next call
*    X - thread's reentry point
*
* Thread element:
*    9,U - delta x (word)
*   11,U - delta y (word)
*   14,U - lifespan
*

14A8:AE 47		LDX   7,U
14AA:EC 02		LDD   2,X	; get current raster
14AC:C3 00 04		ADDD  #$0004	; advance to next
14AF:10 83 1A 40	CMPD  #$1A40	; past the last?
14B3:23 03		BLS   $14B8

14B5:CC 1A 34		LDD   #$1A34	; yes, restart from first raster
14B8:ED 02		STD   2,X	; save new raster

14BA:EC 0E		LDD   14,X	; fetch xc
14BC:E3 49		ADDD  9,U	; add delta x
14BE:ED 0E		STD   14,X	; store back
14C0:EC 88 10		LDD   16,X	; get yc
14C3:E3 4B		ADDD  11,U	; add delta y
14C5:ED 88 10		STD   16,X	; store back
14C8:6A 4E		DEC   14,U	; drop lifespan
14CA:27 08		BEQ   $14D4	; dead, so remove

14CC:86 04		LDA   #$04	; when to return
14CE:8E 14 A8		LDX   #$14A8	; where to return to
14D1:7E D0 66		JMP   $D066	; leave thread

14D4:BD D0 75		JSR   $D075	; remove shape
14D7:0A 8A		DEC   $8A	; decrement number of enforcer sparks on screen
14D9:7E D0 63		JMP   $D063	; remove thread

**********************************************************
*
* Thread installed at 5703
*
* I think this may be the thread that cycles the colors
* for the wowzo effect between levels...?
*
* When the thread is started up, it picks one of the
* twelve color cycling tables declared above and then
* picks a random starting offset in the table.
*
* Then as the thread runs, it increments the offset
* and loads all but the first color with the colors
* in the table starting at the offset. So on the next
* dispatch what was in color $0F is put into color $0E,
* what was in $0E is put into $0D, etc.
*
* In addition, three colors are blasted with black in
* a descending cycle. Colors $05, $0A and $0F get it
* first, then colors $04, $09, and $0E, and so on.
*
* U offsets used:
*    7,U - pointer to start of color cycle
*    9,U - pointer to current location within cycle
*   11,U - single byte 0-4 : the three colors to make black

**********************************************************

* Get random color cycle 0-11 from table at $576D

59B0:10 8E 57 6D	LDY   #$576D
59B4:BD D0 39		JSR   $D039	; random number
59B7:84 0F		ANDA  #$0F
59B9:81 0C		CMPA  #$0C
59BB:24 F7		BCC   $59B4

59BD:48			LSLA
59BE:48			LSLA
59BF:1F 89		TFR   A,B
59C1:AE A5		LDX   B,Y	; point to random color cycle

* Get random offset into the cycle we've picked

59C3:CB 02		ADDB  #$02
59C5:BD D0 39		JSR   $D039	; random number
59C8:A4 A5		ANDA  B,Y
59CA:AF 47		STX   7,U	; store cycle we've picked
59CC:30 86		LEAX  A,X	; and start at a random offset
59CE:AF 49		STX   9,U
					; 11,U is not set because it is range checked later
* thread comes back to here

59D0:AE 49		LDX   9,U	; point to location in current color cycle
59D2:30 01		LEAX  1,X	; next entry
59D4:6D 84		TST   ,X	; end of cycle
59D6:26 02		BNE   $59DA

59D8:AE 47		LDX   7,U	; so start over at beginning
59DA:AF 49		STX   9,U	; save current location

* fill colors $01 to $0F with values starting at current location in cycle

59DC:10 8E 98 01	LDY   #$9801	; point to color $01
59E0:A6 80		LDA   ,X+	; get next entry
59E2:26 04		BNE   $59E8	; not end of cycle

59E4:AE 47		LDX   7,U	; end, so start over at beginning of table
59E6:20 F8		BRA   $59E0


59E8:A7 A0		STA   ,Y+	; store new value for color $01
59EA:10 8C 98 10	CMPY  #$9810	; end of colors?
59EE:25 F0		BCS   $59E0	; nope, set next color

* now blast three of the colors black

59F0:C6 00		LDB   #$00
59F2:A6 4B		LDA   11,U
59F4:4A			DECA		; pick new set of three to make black
59F5:81 05		CMPA  #$05	; big number (rolled over from last dispatch)?
59F7:25 02		BCS   $59FB

59F9:86 04		LDA   #$04	; yes, put into range
59FB:A7 4B		STA   11,U

* 11,U is 4: set colors $05, $0A, $0F to black
* 11,U is 3: set colors $04, $09, $0E to black
* 11,U is 2: set colors $03, $08, $0D to black
* 11,U is 1: set colors $02, $07, $0C to black
* 11,U is 0: set colors $01, $06, $0B to black

59FD:8E 98 01		LDX   #$9801	; point to color $01
5A00:E7 86		STB   A,X	; make it black
5A02:30 05		LEAX  5,X	; do two more, 5 colors apart
5A04:8C 98 10		CMPX  #$9810
5A07:25 F7		BCS   $5A00

5A09:86 01		LDA   #$01
5A0B:8E 59 D0		LDX   #$59D0	; come back to here
5A0E:7E D0 66		JMP   $D066	; leave thread

*
* Startup thread
*
* Eugene Jarvis says this puts up the Robotron splash screen, etc.
*

77A5:BD D0 60		JSR   $D060	; remove all other threads
77A8:0F F4		CLR   $F4
77AA:BD D0 54		JSR   $D054	; install thread
77AD:77 B9				; thread's entry point
77AF:8E 77 E4		LDX   #$77E4	; thread's entry point
77B0:4F			CLRA		; thread's period
77B3:BD D0 5A		JSR   $D05A	; install another thread
77B6:7E D0 63		JMP   $D063	; return and remove this thread
